LAM GYI GZHUNG SHING SMON 'JUG GNYIS, ,LEGS PAR BZUNG NAS JI
LTAR KHAS BLANGS BZHIN, ,RGYAL SRAS SPYOD LA SLOB PA 'DI

MED PAR, ,THAMS CAD MKHYEN PAR 'GRO BA'I LAM YOD PA, ,RGYAL DANG
DE SRAS MKHAS RNAMS MI BZHED KYANG, ,RDO RJE THEG DANG PHA ROL
PHYIN PA LA, ,GNANG BKAG MI 'DRA 'GA' RE GSUNGS PA LA, ,CHES
CHER 'KHRUL ZHING MNGON RLOM GYIS MTHO BA'I, ,SKAL

DMAN RNAMS KYI THEG CHEN SPYI YI GZHUNG, ,DRI MA MED PA'I LAM
BZANG NUB PAR BYAS, ,DE PHYIR RDO RJE THEG PAR 'JUG NA YANG,
,DRI MA MED PA'I MDO SDE RNAMS KYI DON, ,BYAMS PA KLU SGRUB
THOGS MED KYIS BSHAD PA'I, ,BYANG CHUB SEMS BSKYED SDOM PA BZUNG
NAS

@108A *, ,NI; ;PHAR PHYIN DRUG LA SLOB PA GZHIR ZUNG LA, ,RDO
RJE THEG PA'I LAM GYI SNON PA THOB, ,DE NI MA TSANG MED PA'I
THEG MCHOG LAM, ,DE LAS GZHAN RNAMS BYIS PA DGA' SKYED YIN, ,DE
LTAR SRAS BCAS RGYAL BA'I BGROD GCIG LAm,,

RGYAL SRAS SDOM PA DAG PAR BYED PA'I TSUL, ,YID CHES LUNG DANG
DRI MED RIGS PA LAS, ,RNAM PAR BRGAL BA'I RANG BZO'I DRI MA YIS,
,MA BSLAD RGYAL BA'I DGONGS PA JI BZHIN DU, ,GO SLA'I TSIG GIS
RNAM PAR BKRAL BA 'DIS, ,GANG LA RGYUN DU

GUS PA'I MTHUS BYUNG BA, ,'JAM PA'I DBYANGS LA RTAG TU PHYAG
'TSAL LO, ,THEG MCHOG LAM ZAB BDAG BLO BYIS PA'I TSUL, ,DE PHYIR
TSIG DANG DON LA SKYON CHAGS NA, ,'PHAGS DANG MKHAS PA'I SPYAN
SNGAR BDAG 'CHAGS KYIS, ,BRTZE LDAN RNAmS

KYIS NONGS DA BZLOG TU GSOL, ,THUB BSTAN SPYI DANG KHYAD PAR
THEG MCHOG GI ,LAM GYI SROG RNAMS PHAL CHER NUB PA YI, ,TSUL 'DI
MTHONG NAS BSTAN PA GNAS BYA'I PHYIR, ,DE LTAR 'BAD LAS DGE BA
GANG BSAGS PA, ,DE YIS 'GRO KUN LAM

LTAR BCOS PA LA, ,DGA' BA MED CING YANG DAG LAM GYI GNANG,
,RDZOGS PAR MTHONG NAS SGRUB LA BRTZON PAR SHOG ,BDAG KYANG TSE
RABS KUN TU 'JAM PA'I DBYANGS, ,DAM PA'I MGON GYIS BZUNG NAS
THEG PA MCHOG ,TSUL BZHIN RTOGS

NAS 'GRO BA SGROL BA'I KHUR, ,KHYER NAS RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA
RGYAS BYED SHOG ,BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I SDOM PA BZUNG NAS TSUL
KHRIMS KYI PHUNG PO YONGS SU DAG PAR BYA BA'I TSUL RNAM PAR
BSHAD PA BYANG CHUB GZHUNG LAM ZHES BYA BA 'DI NI BYANG CHUB

@108B SEMS DPA'I SKYOD PA LA MOS PA CUNG ZAD SKYES PA SH'AKYA'I
DGE SLONG BLO BZANG GRAGS PA'I DPAL GYIS RGYAL SRAS KYI SDOM PA
BZUNG NAS BSLAB PA LA SLOB PAR 'DOD PA RNAMS KYI DON DU BYANG RA
